                var JsErrorStorage = function () {
                    var storage = [];
                    return {
                        add: function (error) {
                            storage.push(error);
                        },
                        getAll: function () {
                            return storage;
                        }
                    };
                }();
                window.onerror = function (message, url, line, columnNo, error) {
                    if (url != '' && line != 0) {
                        JsErrorStorage.add({message: message, url: url, line: line, columnNo: columnNo, error: error && error.stack});
                    }
                };
            </script>
<script type="text/javascript">
                function useUntil(callback, condition) {
                    if (typeof callback !== 'function') {
                        throw new Error('[useUntil] callback must be type of function');
                    }
                    if (typeof condition !== 'string') {
                        throw new Error('[useUntil] condition must be type of string');
                    }
                    var isOk = eval(condition);
                    if (typeof isOk !== 'boolean') {
                        throw new Error('[useUntil] condition must return boolean when executing');
                    }
                    if (isOk) {
                        callback();
                    } else {
                        setTimeout(function() { useUntil(callback, condition) }, 20);
                    }
                }

                function useJQuery(callback) {
                    useUntil(callback, 'typeof window.jQuery === "function"');
                }
            </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    analyticsEvent = analyticsVPV = analyticsClearVPV = analyticsForm = function () {};
    var googleTrackingParameters = {"page":{"type":"webtv_link","category":"opinion","subcategory":"kommentatorer"},"content":{"video":true,"author":"gauth-tom.jensen","pubdate":1582441200,"title":"\/kommentatorer\/gud-naade-og-troeste-os-hvis-bernie-sanders-bliver-praesident","id":1445434,"length":"1342","source":"int","movieSource":"","paymentModel":"subscription"},"event":"dataLayerPush"};
    var googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts = ["PaywallData","UserInfoData"];

    function setArticleStats() {
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {
            has_audio: 0,
            number_of_links: 5,
            number_of_embeds: 1,
            characters_count: 5840,
        }});
    }

    function setPageType() {
        var pageType = window.dfpConfig.targetingParams.articleType;

        if(pageType) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {page: {type: pageType}});
        }
    }

    var isDataLayerReady = false;
    function setDataLayer() {
        if (googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.length === 0) {
            if (googleTrackingParameters.user && googleTrackingParameters.user.access === undefined) {
                googleTrackingParameters.user.access = 1;
            }

            window.dataLayer.push(googleTrackingParameters);
            isDataLayerReady = true;
            document.dispatchEvent(window.createJSEvent('DataLayerReady'));
        }
    }

    function setUserData() {
        try {
            var userInfo = bpcModule.getUserInfo();

            var reqrole = 'Anonymous';
            var hasSubscription = false;

            if (userInfo.roles !== undefined) {
                reqrole = userInfo.roles.join(',');
                hasSubscription = userInfo.roles.indexOf('ROLE_USER_PLUS_MEMBER') >= 0;
            }

            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: mapUserData(userInfo)});
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {reqrole: reqrole}});

            if(!!googleTrackingParameters.content.paywall && hasSubscription) {
                googleTrackingParameters.user.access = 1;
                googleTrackingParameters.content.paywall = null;
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("GTM tracking issue", e);
        }
        removeElementFromArray('UserInfoData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
        setDataLayer();
    }

    function mapUserData(userInfo) {
        var userData = {
            'id': (userInfo.userId !== undefined) ? userInfo.userId : null,
            'auth': ((userInfo.userId !== undefined) && (userInfo.userId !== null)) ? 1 : 0,
            'gigyaID': (userInfo.gigyaUserId !== undefined) ? userInfo.gigyaUserId : null
        };
        if (userInfo.subscriptionType !== undefined && userInfo.subscriptionType !== null) {
            userData.subscriptionType = userInfo.subscriptionType;
        }
        return userData;
    }

    function removeElementFromArray(value, array) {
        index = array.indexOf(value);
        if (index !== -1) {
            array.splice(index, 1);
        }
    }

    function setAdblockData() {
        if (typeof adblockJsFile === 'undefined') {
            adblockJsFile = 0;
        }
        $.extend(googleTrackingParameters, {
            adblock: !adblockJsFile
        });
        removeElementFromArray('AdblockData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
    }

    function setPaywallData(event, $paywallData) {
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: {access: $paywallData.access ? 1 : 0}});

        if ($paywallData.type) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {paywall: $paywallData.type}});
        }
        if ($paywallData.paymentModel) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {paymentModel: $paywallData.paymentModel}});
        }

        removeElementFromArray('PaywallData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
        setDataLayer();
    }

    var wasDataLayerInited = false;
    function initializeDataLayer() {
        if (wasDataLayerInited === true) {
            return;
        }

        if(!googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.includes('UserInfoData')) {
          setUserData();
        }

        setArticleStats();
        setAdblockData();
        setPageType();
        setDataLayer();
        wasDataLayerInited = true;
    }

    var onDataLayerReady = function (callback) {
        if(isDataLayerReady) {
            callback();
        } else {
            document.addEventListener("DataLayerReady", callback);
        }
    }

    useJQuery(function () {
        if(googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.includes('UserInfoData')) {
            window.bpcModule.initialize().finally(setUserData);
        }

        initializeDataLayer();
        $(document).on('PaywallInitialized', setPaywallData);
        $(document).on('BeM_Cookiebot_Ready BeM_Document_Ready', function () {
            initializeDataLayer();
        });
        $(document).on('loginSuccess logout', setUserData);
    });
</script>

    var min = date.getUTCMinutes();
    if (min < 10) {
        min = "0" + min;

<h1 class="article-header__title" data-paywall-flow-anchor="">Gud nåde og trøste os, hvis Bernie Sanders bliver præsident</h1>
<p class="article-header__intro">Måske skulle også den danske venstrefløj vare sig med helgenkåringen af Sanders; uanset hvor lidt man måtte bryde sig om Trump. Sanders kan være præcis det alternativ, som er betydeligt værre. Også for os i Europa og i Danmark. </p>
</header>

    (function insertJwPlayerScript() {
        var baseUrl = 'https://content.jwplatform.com/libraries/',
            playerIds = {"mobile":"JxbA9fSq","tablet":"Lifycoa2","desktop":"l1NZ7tzm"},
            playerId = playerIds.desktop || '',
            playerElementId = 'mediaplayer-1445434-1135826455';

        var path = (function resolvePath() {
            if (window.md !== undefined) {
                if (window.md.phone()) {
                    playerId = playerIds.mobile;
                } else if (window.md.tablet()) {
                    playerId = playerIds.tablet;
                }
            }
            if (baseUrl !== '' && playerId !== '') {
                return baseUrl + playerId + '.js';
            }
            return '';
        }());

        if (path) {
            var jwPlayerScript = document.createElement('script');
            jwPlayerScript.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
            jwPlayerScript.setAttribute('src', path);

            var thisScript = document.getElementById('jwplayer-resolve-' + playerElementId);
            thisScript.parentNode.insertBefore(jwPlayerScript, thisScript.nextSibling);
        }
    })();

                            window.invokeVideoPlayer = function(prerollTag, postrollTag) {
                                if (playerLoaded !== undefined && playerLoaded || prerollTag === false && postrollTag === false) {
                                    return;
                                }
                                if (waitForBidsTimeout !== undefined) {
                                    clearTimeout(waitForBidsTimeout);
                                }
                                if (prerollAdvertisementUrl !== undefined) {
                                    prerollAdvertisementUrl = prerollTag;
                                }
                                if (postrollAdvertisementUrl !== undefined) {
                                    postrollAdvertisementUrl = postrollTag;
                                }

                            };

                            if (!playerLoaded && (typeof prerollTag !== 'undefined' && prerollTag || typeof postrollTag !== 'undefined' && postrollTag)) {

                                const playerContainer = document.getElementById('mediaplayer-1445434-1135826455');
                                playerContainer.style.margin = '0 auto';
                                playerContainer.parentElement.style.backgroundColor = '#000';
                            }

                            function aspectRatio(width, height) {
                                let ratio = width / height;
                                if (ratio < 1.7 && ratio > 1) {
                                    return {
                                        width: "100%",
                                        stretching: "none"
                                    };
                                } else if (ratio === 1) {
                                    return {
                                        aspectratio: "1:1"
                                    };
                                } else if (ratio < 1) {

                                    if (window.md.phone()) {
                                        return {
                                          stretching: "uniform",
                                          aspectratio: width + ":" + height
                                        };
                                    } else {
                                        fitVerticalVideo();
                                        return {
                                          stretching: "uniform",
                                          width: "50%",
                                          aspectratio: width + ":" + height
                                        };
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    return {
                                        aspectratio: width + ":" + height
                                    };
                                }
                            }

                                                                                                                            image: "https://berlingske.bmcdn.dk/media/cache/resolve/image_620x350/image/126/1263006/23349844-tom-jensen.jpg",
                                                                                events: {
                                            visualQuality: function(e) {
                                                if (e.level && e.level.width) {
                                                    this.setConfig(
                                                        aspectRatio(e.level.width, e.level.height)
                                                    );
                                                }
                                            }
                                        },
                                                                                                                                        advertising: {
                                                    client: "googima",
                                                    schedule: {
                                                        preroll: {
                                                            tag: prerollAdvertisementUrl,
                                                            offset: "pre"
                                                            },
                                                        postroll: {
                                                            tag: postrollAdvertisementUrl,
                                                            offset: "post"
                                                        }
                                                    },
                                                    skipoffset: 10000,
                                                    vpaidcontrols: true,
                                                },
                                                                                    
    skin: {
        name: "berlingske"
    },
    controls: true,
                    image: "https://berlingske.bmcdn.dk/media/cache/resolve/image_1230x692_jwplayer_thumbnail/image/126/1263006/23349844-tom-jensen.jpg",
        playlist: "//content.jwplatform.com/v2/media/IAwU4y3B",
    localization: {
        nextUp: "Se også"
    },
                                    }
                                };

                                const initPlayer = function () {
                                    if ('function' !== typeof jwplayer) {
                                        setTimeout(initPlayer, 100);
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    Video.initializeJWVideo(jwData, true);
                                };

                                initPlayer();
                            };
                        });
                    </script>
</div>
</figure>
</div>
</div>
</div>

            var cookieBotEventsSent = false;
            var pushCookieBotEvents = function () {
                if (cookieBotEventsSent !== false) {
                    return;
                }
                cookieBotEventsSent = true;
                if (Cookiebot.consent.preferences) {
                    window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'cookieconsent_preferences'});
                }
                if (Cookiebot.consent.statistics) {
                    window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'cookieconsent_statistics'});
                }
                if (Cookiebot.consent.marketing) {
                    window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'cookieconsent_marketing'});
                }

                if(typeof Cookiebot.runScripts == "function") {
                  Cookiebot.runScripts();
                }
            };

            $(document).on('BeM_Cookiebot_Ready', function () {
              if(typeof Cookiebot.runScripts === "function") {
                Cookiebot.runScripts();
              }

              onDataLayerReady(() => pushCookieBotEvents());
            })

        </script>
